A classic LA walk up burger joint. While the character of the neighborhood seems run down the cook was pleasant and attentive. The burger was flavourful and cooked well with plenty of fresh toppings. "Mr. Grumpy" greets you with a sinister smile...asking which "killer" meal fills your death wish best...hamburger or pastrami?
Met a man at the window who  drove in from Orange County to satisfy his CRAVING. He was in his late 40's and came here with his Dad as a youngster.
He said pastrami just doesn't taste the same anywhere else...and "yes" he knew it was "bad for him."
I believe in moderation, we can enjoy some of the "forbiddins' of life" but this is ridiculous...I mean really! It should at least taste good going down.
In today's world...it's amazing this "glutten haven" is still around.
The "burger" I tried to eat was hard grill fried in old, old greese...(It's part of their "flavoring" experience...I guess) on a small old, old bun.
It turned out, it was good I couldn't get it all down...what I did came back up all day. Nasty business!
On my 10 Worst List!<//text>

<text>My dad used to bring me here when I was a little kid along with the Original Fat Burger and both locations have a lot of...charisma and flavor. Yet this one is still standing.

I usually got the steak sandwich with fries that came in the bottom half of a cardboard box...remember charisma. If memory serves correct it was always delicious and greasy but not the most tender cut of meat.

Now to the present: I got a good ol hamburger.
All I can say is fresh, hot, delicious and juicy.
No crazy sauces or buzz ingredients.

The location is divey, I mean charismatic, from the kitchen to the local crowd and maybe some patrons. I don't mind, this is an LA landmark in my opinion. Simple fresh cooking.

Just as a friendly reminder: You may be asked for change or even dollars by some of the locals.<//text><pictures>None<//pictures>< response>

<rating>2< /rating>< review>
I have had a very heartbreaking experience with this pet hospital and will never return.
I brought my kitty in for a routine dental cleaning and let the vet know he is a fearful kitty, which was also apparent during the examination, and was assured they are used to dealing with these situations and everything would be fine, then seemed to rush me out of there.  When I brought him home after the procedure and he was out of his carrier, I saw broken bleeding claws, and a limp tail that dragged on the floor when he tried to take a couple of steps before laying down again in pain.  I immediately called this vet back WHO finally told me he had gotten away and they had to use force to catch him.  I found it disturbing that they made no mention of this incident when I picked him up.  My kitty ended up with a paralized tail, and was put under anesthesia over again by this vet for further tests to try to correct the problem, never testing him to see if he would have a reaction to the anesthesia that I thought was excessive.  They simply told me they had to protect their staff by using anesthesia over again.  Just a couple of weeks later, my kitty was having trouble breathing, so I rushed him to All Care Pet Emergency Hospital in Fountain Valley, where he was immediately placed into an oxygen tank and kept there for 3 days!  The first night I brought him there, I was told by the attending physician to say my goodbyes because he may not make it through the night, plus I had to sign all these forms authorizing them to resessitate him during the night if while they were treating him.  After a sleepless night and lots of prayers , he made it through this ordeal,
but now he has a permanent irreversible breathing problem, where I have to be prepared to rush him back to emergency should he have trouble breathing again.  This little kitty was healthy, happy, playful and just a sweet baby before this incident, and would never hurt anyone, but who just happened to be afraid of the vet.  He has now lost that playful spirit.  It may be just "another" cat to some people, but he is like a child and loved so much.< /review>

< Review>
I wrote a review for this vet on yelp but I hate that site because the moment I don't log in for more than a few weeks they filter my review.  SO annoying.

This is absolutely the best vet I've had since I moved to CA 12 years ago and said goodbye to the vet I had in Texas.  Dr. Lizardo and Dr. Hashimoto are a kind young married couple who LOVE their patients and know their owners by name and face.  This is every sense of the word "family practice".  We've been coming here for about 6 years.  These two doctors treated my sister's cat for her kidney disease and we kept little Deeda going for about a year before it was her time.  They took care of my cat Kiki from age 14 to age 20... and I drove all the way back from Fresno when I had been living there with a guy in order for them to take a last look at her when she was sick and be the ones to be with me and her in her last moments.

I now have a new kitty named Charlie and he is 1 year old.  We got him from a rescue shelter and he's the sweetest boy.  However, he would have probably darwinized himself by now if it weren't for Dr. Lizardo.  He's managed to get his tail smashed and need it amputated (the tissue became necrotic beyond where the tail injury was), got his face stunt by a bee and had a reaction, had a fungal infection in his nose, and now he got into my sewing thread when I accidentally left the door open and was gone for a day.  I came back to thread all over the house and thought nothing of it, but the next evening he threw up 12 times and refused to eat and became very lethargic.

Beach Blvd Pet Hospital ALWAYS makes room for your pets when they need to be seen urgently. If it is during office hours they WILL see you if you need them.  Dr. Hashimoto examined Charlie and was concerned for his reaction to his tummy exam so they did an X-ray and found nothing.  The two Dr's discussed the situation and suggested to me that they do exploratory surgery.  It wasn't cheap, but it was MUCH cheaper than it would have been at somewhere like VCA or one of the big fancy clinics.  I asked them to do it after he explained to me the reason why it was necessary, and SURE ENOUGH... Dr. Lizardo found 3 FEET of black thread coiled up in his small intestine.  He would have died a few days later from the string getting stuck in his intestines and causing them to shift and bunch up.  What a horrible way for a sweet animal to die.  If it wasn't for Dr. Lizardo's quick thinking he would not have made it.

I am so glad to have this vet.  There are many times in which I have lived all over Southern California (Pasadena, Van Nuys, Monrovia, LA) and I always would be willing to drive 100+ miles to this vet to have these Dr's see my pets.  I even did it when I lived in Fresno.  Bring your pet here.  Don't let the small and slightly old look of this place turn you away and send you to some fancy place.  Interior design doesn't make a good vet.  How they treat your animals does, and how they save your animals and make them better.

Once again, thank you guys from the bottom of my heart!!!!< /Review>

<review>I went into Fantazy Motorsports with a rather limited imagination and a set of requests that, while complex, was not something out of range for most after-market and advanced auto customization shops.
In the end, what they gave me wasn't a simple retail purchase, it was quite frankly a work of totally individualized art.
I'm twice as shocked and satisfied by the final product as I had imagined in the best case scenario.
In every element where I had set specifications, they exceeded my requests in both style and quality.
On many things I simply asked Zach and Steve to do what they thought might be best, and so I had many wonderful surprises when I picked the car up.
In addition to undertaking a massive project and discounting the rates, they fixed my bumper scratches, replaced lighting systems, designed and installed a custom shocks system, created a flush design concept to conceal massively altered systems and air compression components, entirely required four doors, and probably 3 other things in forgetting all free of charge by the shop.
Additonally, Walter was able to design and install a sound system that exceeds in power and crispness anything that I have ever heard. Words can't express the way that his personal refinement literally produced sound that delved into the core of your bones and came out your skin with pulsating physical and auditory sensation that does defy description.
Not ashamed to say that in my surprise and delight when I picked it up, elements of the sound system, air suspension, concave rim fits, exhaust adjustments, trunk concealment, lighting package, and exterior trim modifications had me literally a little teary-eyed with gratitude.
And I smiled with amazement as the entire crew checked the vehicle over, with co-owner George checking every minute detail. And co-owner Freddie later taking some amazing photographs.
In the weeks since I left I've been trying to think of reasons to get back in there but my car is perfectly perfect (for now)!
Thanks you Steve, Zach, Walter, Junior, Memo, George, Freddie and the rest of your crew!!!< /review>< Pics>

<review>Car Audio is exciting. But also prone to sneaky oil sales man, botched installs, delays and bad customer service. You get what you pay for and Fantazy Motorsports Team of Zach, Steve, Aurian and Momo really came through here.

Im very picky on who I let touch my 2014 Porsche 911 S convertible.
I compared feedback on rennlist and 6speed forums, read through a dozen places yelp reviews. Some are great if you want a new HU in your Camry but not so great when it comes to high end cars. Steve (Manager) was super knowledgable, personal and calm. He explained pros and cons of each component, suggested but not pressured me into buying or upgrading anything. Im very impressed by his demeanor and the whole crews attitude towards perfection. As a German that means a lot to me.

Zach replied to my inquiry email within 20 minutes, he always knew the status of this and that and made me feel comfortable I was a human being not a number in their system.

Steve called JL Audio and Audison several times over the course of this build. He suggested replacement of speakers for a better performance, like 2 x 10inch thin Subwoofers in custom build ported stealth box for my backseat as opposed to one 12 inch full size sub that would stand out.

Mom took over an hour sitting in the car with me with his laptop to adjust and tune the Audisson DSP to my liking.

Aurian detailed my car and went to great lengths to explain what ceramic coating does and does not do. He even paint corrected a fender to show what exactly I could expect which detail, detail + paint correct and ceramic coat on top. I was telling him I understood, but he insisted on finished that panel as it drive him crazy otherwise! Thats my kid of crazy!

Point being they know their stuff, they do it well and you will be happy you went here. I drove 2 hours from the Southbay to Thousand Oaks as they are the most recommended porsche car audio shop in southern CA.
And since I went all Active on my speakers I wanted the best!

Ultimately I upgraded my Bose Amp + Speakers as well as my PCM headhunt with this:

Pioneer AVICW8400NEX (Wireless Apple Carplay)
Backup Camera
Front STAGE:
HERTZ MILLE LEGEND ML280.3  1.1INCH Tweeter
HERTZ MILLE LEGEND ML700.3  3 INCH Midbass
HERTZ MILLE LEGEND ML1650.3  6.5 INCH Woofer

Subwoofer in custom stealth ported Enclosure:
2x JL Audio 10TW3-D4 10 inch subwoofer

Amps: Alpine PDX V9+ and Sound Digital 400.4DEVO4
driving all Speakers active(!) through an Audison Bit NOVE DSP

I like Classical, Rock, Metal, Jazz, Blues and some electro. I do not care for Rap/Hip-Hop or dubstep. I wanted tight, strong, low bass. Not booming, not SPL window shatter but a setup that can keep up with super fast double bassdrums in metal songs as well as high pitched Trumpets, Horns, Cimbals, Triangles, Fluets, Violins and female Vocals.
Im blown away by the system and its still breaking in!

A super big thank you to all the hard working crew at Fantazy Motorsport! Please reach out to me on Yelp if you want anymore details.

<name>Sheila Albertson< /name>< text>
Fantastic customer service from the ladies at the register. It was our first visit and they took the time to explain the ordering and make recommendations. They use peanut oil and have bins of free peanuts to snack on which is a nice touch.

The restaurant is new and pretty clean. The bathrooms were spotless. It wasn't too busy at lunch on a Saturday, and the wait for food was only about five minutes.

The fries are delicious and come out piping hot! They are heavy handed with the salt, so if you're sensitive you may want to make a special request.

My daughter loved the plain ketchup hot dog. My husband had a bacon burger with mushrooms that was great. My cheeseburger was just ok. The meat patty was well seasoned and it came out hot. My complaint is there was only a scant bit of BBQ sauce. I had to look to see if it was added because I didn't taste it in the first bite, so only 3-stars for now.<//text>

< text>
This was my first visit to this burger chain that has seemingly unseated In-n-out as the nations most popular.
The service was great. The young lady that helped us was patient in explaining the menu board, so we were able to make a choice.
I chose to have my burger the same way I get it from In-n-out so I could easily compare.
The good thing about Five guys, even though it's a little more expensive is that the burger is more substantial and therefore I felt more satisfied.
And it was a tasty burger (read that with Sam Jackson's voice in mind).  And I also think I might like the fries better.
But to be honest, the In-n-out burger is more flavorful. In-n-out actually makes you want another burger, which is a good strategy.
But the Five Guys burger makes you feel like you wanna come back...on another day.
And I will be back.
But, no offense to this particular location, I'm still a In-n-out guy.</text>

< review>
This was my first experience at Five Guys. I went in with very high expectations because I've heard some hype over the last year or so. The menu is fairly simply but ordering is not very streamlined. The burgers are also confusing for a first-timer. A "little burger" just means one Patty and a "bib burger" means two patties. Seems like an odd way to market ones food. I wanted one patty but ordering a little burger seemed like I was asking for something I didn't want. Anyway, burger was good, definitely didn't live up to the hype. The staff was friendly and the price was reasonable. In the future I think I'll just drive past and go to In'N'Out (or even Carl's Jr).<//review>
